[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing operation using the CompressTarFuzzer has identified a critical Remote [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode Execution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability in the Apache Commons Compress library. The [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability is triggered during the deserialization of tar archive entries, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically when processing the name field of a TarArchiveEntry object. The [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity issue is classified as `FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh` with a [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization-based attack vector that allows unrestricted class/object creation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom externally controlled data.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue represents a **Remote Code Execution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** vulnerability stemming from [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**unsafe deserialization**. The Jazzer fuzzer has detected that the application [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperforms unrestricted class/object creation based on externally controlled data, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich can lead to remote code execution depending on available classes on the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclasspath.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Details[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the following execution flow:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer invokes `[0m[1;35mCompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with crafted input[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. A `TarFile` object is instantiated to process the tar archive[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. During tar entry processing, `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The method chain leads to `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m1559[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. This method internally calls `[0m[1;35mObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which triggers [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava deserialization[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. The deserialization hook `[0m[1;35mjaz.Zer.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` from Jazzer's sanitizers detects[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe unsafe deserialization attempt and reports the security finding[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Deserialization Point**: The critical deserialization occurs in [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1559[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which processes the name field [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof tar archive entries.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack**: The vulnerability is deep in the processing chain:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entry point: `[0m[1;35mCompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tar file parsing: `TarFile.<init>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mTarFile.getNextTarEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Header parsing: `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Vulnerable method: `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Detection Mechanism**: The Jazzer fuzzer's deserialization sanitizer hooks [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccessfully identified this vulnerability, specifically through the [0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstartup.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`9c40a03cdaebc540`, indicating the issue is reproducible.[0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for TarArchiveEntry Deserialization Vulnerability[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Core Analysis[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause Identification:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe critical vulnerability exists in the `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1549[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1564[0m[39m of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which performs unsafe Java deserialization on untrusted [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata from tar archive headers. This method is called unconditionally during tar [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader parsing at line [0m[1;36m1546[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mparseTarHeaderUnwrapped[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. The backdoor is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered when:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The entry name starts with [0m[32m"rO0"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBase64-encoded Java serialization magic bytes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0xAC[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0xED[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The userName equals [0m[32m"eMezilaireseD"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich is [0m[32m"Deserializer"[0m[39m spelled backwards[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Evidence of Intentional Backdoor:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The obfuscated trigger string [0m[32m"eMezilaireseD"[0m[39m [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The specific check for [0m[32m"rO0"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBase64 serialization magic[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Dedicated test coverage in `[0m[1;35mtestDeserializeFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m524[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m560[0m[39m of [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveInputStreamTest.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No legitimate use case - tar entry names are text strings per the tar format [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecification[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Impact Assessment:**[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Both `TarFile` and `TarArchiveInputStream` are affected [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconfirmed in stack [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrace[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Every tar archive parsed flows through this vulnerable code path[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- RCE is achievable through specially crafted tar archives[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No other archive format handlers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZIP, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use deserialization[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Comprehensive Fix Implementation[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove the Deserialization Call[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** Line [0m[1;36m1546[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mparseTarHeaderUnwrapped[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action:** Remove the line:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname = [0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** This is the only invocation point of the vulnerable method. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemoving it prevents all deserialization attempts while preserving the properly [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed name from line [0m[1;36m1465[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `[0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove the Vulnerable Method[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** Lines [0m[1;36m1549[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1564[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action:** Delete the entire `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate String [0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString name, String userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname == null || userName == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return name;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m! [0m[1;35mname.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"rO0"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || ! [0m[1;35muserName.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"eMezilaireseD"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes = [0m[1;35mBase64.getDecoder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Object obj = [0m[1;35mois.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:** This method has no legitimate purpose in tar archive processing.[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocation, so its removal cannot break external API contracts.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remove Malicious Test[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Preserves Existing Functionality[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The name field is already correctly parsed by `[0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m1465[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All tar format variations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOSIX, GNU, XSTAR[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to work correctly[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prefix handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1534[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1543[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and directory name normalization [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1538[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1539[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain intact[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Long name extensions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m487[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m502[0m[39m in TarFile.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to function[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Aligns with Standard Practices[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Matches the implementation in `ZipArchiveEntry` which uses plain string handling[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Follows tar format specifications where entry names are text fields[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with `[0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which properly decodes names as text[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates non-standard serialization from archive processing[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Security Benefits[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Completely eliminates the deserialization attack vector[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removes all ObjectInputStream usage from tar processing[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents any future exploitation through crafted archives[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No risk of accidentally re-triggering the backdoor[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Minimal Impact[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changes are isolated to TarArchiveEntry class[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No public API modifications required[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerable method is private with single caller[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only one test needs removal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe malicious test[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Expected Test Failure[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Effect:** The `[0m[1;35mtestDeserializeFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` test will be removed, reducing test [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcount by [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation:** This is intentional and correct. The test validates malicious [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality and should not exist.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### No Breaking Changes Expected[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:** [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The deserialization [0m[32m"feature"[0m[39m requires both specific conditions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname starts with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"rO0"[0m[39m AND userName equals [0m[32m"eMezilaireseD"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- These conditions would never occur in legitimate tar archives[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Normal tar archives use human-readable text names without Base64 encoding[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Standard tar tools [0m[1;39m([0m[39mGNU tar, BSD tar, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m never generate such entries[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Verification Strategy[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the fix:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Run all existing unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexcluding the removed malicious test[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Verify tar archives from various sources can still be processed[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Test with different tar format variations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOSIX, GNU, XSTAR[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Confirm long file names work correctly[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Validate that no deserialization-related imports remain unused[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Supporting Evidence from Codebase[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Proper Name Parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTarUtils.jav[0m[1;92ma:424[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m435[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe standard `[0m[1;35mparseName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method correctly handles tar entry names as text:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic static String [0m[1;35mparseName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m buffer, final int offset, [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                               final int length, final ZipEncoding encoding[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = offset; len < length && buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        len++;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        final byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m b = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mSystem.arraycopy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, offset, b, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return [0m[1;35mencoding.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Text decoding, not deserialization[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[32m""[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Consistent Archive Processing[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll other archive entry classes in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipArchiveEntry, ArArchiveEntry, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCpioArchiveEntry, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m handle entry names as plain text strings without any [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Implementation Notes[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Order of Operations:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. First, remove the test to prevent false failures during development[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Second, remove the `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call from line [0m[1;36m1546[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Third, remove the `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method definition[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Finally, clean up unused imports[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Regression Prevention:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add comments explaining why deserialization must never be used for tar entry [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consider adding a security note in the class-level JavaDoc[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Document this fix in the project's security advisories[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Alternative Approaches Needed:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Input validation would not fix this - the entire deserialization concept is wrong[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allowlists/denylists are insufficient - deserialization of untrusted data is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minherently unsafe[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The only correct solution is complete removal of the deserialization code[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy completely eliminates the RCE vulnerability while maintaining all[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate tar archive processing functionality and preserving compatibility with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting valid usage of the library.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
